The extension finds images on web pages that do not have any \"alt text\", i.e., captions provided for the image by the web page author. When it finds such an image, it sends the image's source (i.e., URL) to a web service. That web service uses the Bing Image Search API to request both a caption and known web pages containing the same image (or related image). Any captions found are sent back to the extension to be added as the \"alt text\" for the image so that a screen reader can read it. Captions are either those returned by the Bing service or else were found by the service from parsing the pages returned by the Bing service.\r\n","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9PN36R9NBTRM","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Keep docs.microsoft.com in English","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.29991.14352039980302430.1fc81fbd-4756-45c1-93c8-d58027fe8ac2.bd4ddcf0-05c7-4232-a2fc-8921fa2d4348","Height":150,"Width":150,"BackgroundColor":"transparent","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Gratis","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["52364RenSpik.26312AF892AB1_8nvkw576ypakw"],"ContentIds":["7611ba80-c959-a0f1-6c7f-b9eea7ecce5e"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Redirects from machine translated docs.microsoft.com to English version.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9PJ1T0X6GDQS","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"My Podcast -
